\DoxyCodeLine{00581\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ the\ array\ syntax\ is\ just\ a\ way\ to\ document\ the\ number\ of\ elements\ that\ are\ expected\ to\ be\ accessible.\ You\ can\ pass\ address\ of\ your\ first\ element\ out\ of\ a\ contiguous\ set,\ e.g.\ \&myvector.x}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00582\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ -\/\ Adjust\ format\ string\ to\ decorate\ the\ value\ with\ a\ prefix,\ a\ suffix,\ or\ adapt\ the\ editing\ and\ display\ precision\ e.g.\ "{}\%.3f"{}\ -\/>\ 1.234;\ "{}\%5.2f\ secs"{}\ -\/>\ 01.23\ secs;\ "{}Biscuit:\ \%.0f"{}\ -\/>\ Biscuit:\ 1;\ etc.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00583\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ -\/\ Format\ string\ may\ also\ be\ set\ to\ NULL\ or\ use\ the\ default\ format\ ("{}\%f"{}\ or\ "{}\%d"{}).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00584\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ -\/\ Speed\ are\ per-\/pixel\ of\ mouse\ movement\ (v\_speed=0.2f:\ mouse\ needs\ to\ move\ by\ 5\ pixels\ to\ increase\ value\ by\ 1).\ For\ keyboard/gamepad\ navigation,\ minimum\ speed\ is\ Max(v\_speed,\ minimum\_step\_at\_given\_precision).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00585\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ -\/\ Use\ v\_min\ <\ v\_max\ to\ clamp\ edits\ to\ given\ limits.\ Note\ that\ CTRL+Click\ manual\ input\ can\ override\ those\ limits\ if\ ImGuiSliderFlags\_AlwaysClamp\ is\ not\ used.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00586\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ -\/\ Use\ v\_max\ =\ FLT\_MAX\ /\ INT\_MAX\ etc\ to\ avoid\ clamping\ to\ a\ maximum,\ same\ with\ v\_min\ =\ -\/FLT\_MAX\ /\ INT\_MIN\ to\ avoid\ clamping\ to\ a\ minimum.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00587\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ -\/\ We\ use\ the\ same\ sets\ of\ flags\ for\ DragXXX()\ and\ SliderXXX()\ functions\ as\ the\ features\ are\ the\ same\ and\ it\ makes\ it\ easier\ to\ swap\ them.}}

\DoxyCodeLine{00747\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ Popups,\ Modals}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00748\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ -\/\ They\ block\ normal\ mouse\ hovering\ detection\ (and\ therefore\ most\ mouse\ interactions)\ behind\ them.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00749\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ -\/\ If\ not\ modal:\ they\ can\ be\ closed\ by\ clicking\ anywhere\ outside\ them,\ or\ by\ pressing\ ESCAPE.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00750\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ -\/\ Their\ visibility\ state\ (\string~bool)\ is\ held\ internally\ instead\ of\ being\ held\ by\ the\ programmer\ as\ we\ are\ used\ to\ with\ regular\ Begin*()\ calls.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00751\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ -\/\ The\ 3\ properties\ above\ are\ related:\ we\ need\ to\ retain\ popup\ visibility\ state\ in\ the\ library\ because\ popups\ may\ be\ closed\ as\ any\ time.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00752\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ -\/\ You\ can\ bypass\ the\ hovering\ restriction\ by\ using\ ImGuiHoveredFlags\_AllowWhenBlockedByPopup\ when\ calling\ IsItemHovered()\ or\ IsWindowHovered().}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00753\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ -\/\ IMPORTANT:\ Popup\ identifiers\ are\ relative\ to\ the\ current\ ID\ stack,\ so\ OpenPopup\ and\ BeginPopup\ generally\ needs\ to\ be\ at\ the\ same\ level\ of\ the\ stack.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00754\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ This\ is\ sometimes\ leading\ to\ confusing\ mistakes.\ May\ rework\ this\ in\ the\ future.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00755\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ -\/\ BeginPopup():\ query\ popup\ state,\ if\ open\ start\ appending\ into\ the\ window.\ Call\ EndPopup()\ afterwards\ if\ returned\ true.\ ImGuiWindowFlags\ are\ forwarded\ to\ the\ window.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00756\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ -\/\ BeginPopupModal():\ block\ every\ interaction\ behind\ the\ window,\ cannot\ be\ closed\ by\ user,\ add\ a\ dimming\ background,\ has\ a\ title\ bar.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00757\ \ \ \ \ IMGUI\_API\ \textcolor{keywordtype}{bool}\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ BeginPopup(const\ \textcolor{keywordtype}{char}*\ str\_id,\ ImGuiWindowFlags\ flags\ =\ 0);\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ return\ true\ if\ the\ popup\ is\ open,\ and\ you\ can\ start\ outputting\ to\ it.}}

\DoxyCodeLine{00789\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ Tables}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00790\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ -\/\ Full-\/featured\ replacement\ for\ old\ Columns\ API.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00791\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ -\/\ See\ Demo-\/>Tables\ for\ demo\ code.\ See\ top\ of\ imgui\_tables.cpp\ for\ general\ commentary.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00792\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ -\/\ See\ ImGuiTableFlags\_\ and\ ImGuiTableColumnFlags\_\ enums\ for\ a\ description\ of\ available\ flags.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00793\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ The\ typical\ call\ flow\ is:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00794\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ -\/\ 1.\ Call\ BeginTable(),\ early\ out\ if\ returning\ false.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00795\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ -\/\ 2.\ Optionally\ call\ TableSetupColumn()\ to\ submit\ column\ name/flags/defaults.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00796\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ -\/\ 3.\ Optionally\ call\ TableSetupScrollFreeze()\ to\ request\ scroll\ freezing\ of\ columns/rows.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00797\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ -\/\ 4.\ Optionally\ call\ TableHeadersRow()\ to\ submit\ a\ header\ row.\ Names\ are\ pulled\ from\ TableSetupColumn()\ data.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00798\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ -\/\ 5.\ Populate\ contents:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00799\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ -\/\ In\ most\ situations\ you\ can\ use\ TableNextRow()\ +\ TableSetColumnIndex(N)\ to\ start\ appending\ into\ a\ column.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00800\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ -\/\ If\ you\ are\ using\ tables\ as\ a\ sort\ of\ grid,\ where\ every\ column\ is\ holding\ the\ same\ type\ of\ contents,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00801\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ \ \ you\ may\ prefer\ using\ TableNextColumn()\ instead\ of\ TableNextRow()\ +\ TableSetColumnIndex().}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00802\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ \ \ TableNextColumn()\ will\ automatically\ wrap-\/around\ into\ the\ next\ row\ if\ needed.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00803\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ -\/\ IMPORTANT:\ Comparatively\ to\ the\ old\ Columns()\ API,\ we\ need\ to\ call\ TableNextColumn()\ for\ the\ first\ column!}}

\DoxyCodeLine{01105\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ (Legacy:\ bit\ 0\ must\ always\ correspond\ to\ ImGuiChildFlags\_Borders\ to\ be\ backward\ compatible\ with\ old\ API\ using\ 'bool\ border\ =\ false'.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01106\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ About\ using\ AutoResizeX/AutoResizeY\ flags:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01107\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ -\/\ May\ be\ combined\ with\ SetNextWindowSizeConstraints()\ to\ set\ a\ min/max\ size\ for\ each\ axis\ (see\ "{}Demo-\/>Child-\/>Auto-\/resize\ with\ Constraints"{}).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01108\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ -\/\ Size\ measurement\ for\ a\ given\ axis\ is\ only\ performed\ when\ the\ child\ window\ is\ within\ visible\ boundaries,\ or\ is\ just\ appearing.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01109\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ -\/\ This\ allows\ BeginChild()\ to\ return\ false\ when\ not\ within\ boundaries\ (e.g.\ when\ scrolling),\ which\ is\ more\ optimal.\ BUT\ it\ won't\ update\ its\ auto-\/size\ while\ clipped.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01110\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ \ While\ not\ perfect,\ it\ is\ a\ better\ default\ behavior\ as\ the\ always-\/on\ performance\ gain\ is\ more\ valuable\ than\ the\ occasional\ "{}resizing\ after\ becoming\ visible\ again"{}\ glitch.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01111\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ -\/\ You\ may\ also\ use\ ImGuiChildFlags\_AlwaysAutoResize\ to\ force\ an\ update\ even\ when\ child\ window\ is\ not\ in\ view.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01112\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ \ HOWEVER\ PLEASE\ UNDERSTAND\ THAT\ DOING\ SO\ WILL\ PREVENT\ BeginChild()\ FROM\ EVER\ RETURNING\ FALSE,\ disabling\ benefits\ of\ coarse\ clipping.}}

\DoxyCodeLine{01213\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ Flags\ for\ OpenPopup*(),\ BeginPopupContext*(),\ IsPopupOpen()\ functions.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01214\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ -\/\ To\ be\ backward\ compatible\ with\ older\ API\ which\ took\ an\ 'int\ mouse\_button\ =\ 1'\ argument\ instead\ of\ 'ImGuiPopupFlags\ flags',}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01215\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ we\ need\ to\ treat\ small\ flags\ values\ as\ a\ mouse\ button\ index,\ so\ we\ encode\ the\ mouse\ button\ in\ the\ first\ few\ bits\ of\ the\ flags.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01216\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ It\ is\ therefore\ guaranteed\ to\ be\ legal\ to\ pass\ a\ mouse\ button\ index\ in\ ImGuiPopupFlags.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01217\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ -\/\ For\ the\ same\ reason,\ we\ exceptionally\ default\ the\ ImGuiPopupFlags\ argument\ of\ BeginPopupContextXXX\ functions\ to\ 1\ instead\ of\ 0.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01218\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ IMPORTANT:\ because\ the\ default\ parameter\ is\ 1\ (==ImGuiPopupFlags\_MouseButtonRight),\ if\ you\ rely\ on\ the\ default\ parameter}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01219\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ and\ want\ to\ use\ another\ flag,\ you\ need\ to\ pass\ in\ the\ ImGuiPopupFlags\_MouseButtonRight\ flag\ explicitly.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01220\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ -\/\ Multiple\ buttons\ currently\ cannot\ be\ combined/or-\/ed\ in\ those\ functions\ (we\ could\ allow\ it\ later).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01221\ \textcolor{keyword}{enum}\ ImGuiPopupFlags\_}

\DoxyCodeLine{01526\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ and\ prefer\ using\ the\ real\ keys\ (e.g.\ ImGuiKey\_LeftCtrl,\ ImGuiKey\_RightCtrl\ instead\ of\ ImGuiMod\_Ctrl).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01527\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ -\/\ In\ theory\ the\ value\ of\ keyboard\ modifiers\ should\ be\ roughly\ equivalent\ to\ a\ logical\ or\ of\ the\ equivalent\ left/right\ keys.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01528\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ In\ practice:\ it's\ complicated;\ mods\ are\ often\ provided\ from\ different\ sources.\ Keyboard\ layout,\ IME,\ sticky\ keys\ and}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01529\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ backends\ tend\ to\ interfere\ and\ break\ that\ equivalence.\ The\ safer\ decision\ is\ to\ relay\ that\ ambiguity\ down\ to\ the\ end-\/user...}}

\DoxyCodeLine{01868\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ Flags\ for\ ImGui::BeginTable()}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01869\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ -\/\ Important!\ Sizing\ policies\ have\ complex\ and\ subtle\ side\ effects,\ much\ more\ so\ than\ you\ would\ expect.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01870\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ Read\ comments/demos\ carefully\ +\ experiment\ with\ live\ demos\ to\ get\ acquainted\ with\ them.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01871\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ -\/\ The\ DEFAULT\ sizing\ policies\ are:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01872\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ -\/\ Default\ to\ ImGuiTableFlags\_SizingFixedFit\ \ \ \ if\ ScrollX\ is\ on,\ or\ if\ host\ window\ has\ ImGuiWindowFlags\_AlwaysAutoResize.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01873\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ -\/\ Default\ to\ ImGuiTableFlags\_SizingStretchSame\ if\ ScrollX\ is\ off.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01874\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ -\/\ When\ ScrollX\ is\ off:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01875\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ -\/\ Table\ defaults\ to\ ImGuiTableFlags\_SizingStretchSame\ -\/>\ all\ Columns\ defaults\ to\ ImGuiTableColumnFlags\_WidthStretch\ with\ same\ weight.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01876\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ -\/\ Columns\ sizing\ policy\ allowed:\ Stretch\ (default),\ Fixed/Auto.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01877\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ -\/\ Fixed\ Columns\ (if\ any)\ will\ generally\ obtain\ their\ requested\ width\ (unless\ the\ table\ cannot\ fit\ them\ all).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01878\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ -\/\ Stretch\ Columns\ will\ share\ the\ remaining\ width\ according\ to\ their\ respective\ weight.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01879\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ -\/\ Mixed\ Fixed/Stretch\ columns\ is\ possible\ but\ has\ various\ side-\/effects\ on\ resizing\ behaviors.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01880\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ \ \ The\ typical\ use\ of\ mixing\ sizing\ policies\ is:\ any\ number\ of\ LEADING\ Fixed\ columns,\ followed\ by\ one\ or\ two\ TRAILING\ Stretch\ columns.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01881\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ \ \ (this\ is\ because\ the\ visible\ order\ of\ columns\ have\ subtle\ but\ necessary\ effects\ on\ how\ they\ react\ to\ manual\ resizing).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01882\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ -\/\ When\ ScrollX\ is\ on:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01883\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ -\/\ Table\ defaults\ to\ ImGuiTableFlags\_SizingFixedFit\ -\/>\ all\ Columns\ defaults\ to\ ImGuiTableColumnFlags\_WidthFixed}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01884\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ -\/\ Columns\ sizing\ policy\ allowed:\ Fixed/Auto\ mostly.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01885\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ -\/\ Fixed\ Columns\ can\ be\ enlarged\ as\ needed.\ Table\ will\ show\ a\ horizontal\ scrollbar\ if\ needed.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01886\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ -\/\ When\ using\ auto-\/resizing\ (non-\/resizable)\ fixed\ columns,\ querying\ the\ content\ width\ to\ use\ item\ right-\/alignment\ e.g.\ SetNextItemWidth(-\/FLT\_MIN)\ doesn't\ make\ sense,\ would\ create\ a\ feedback\ loop.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01887\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ -\/\ Using\ Stretch\ columns\ OFTEN\ DOES\ NOT\ MAKE\ SENSE\ if\ ScrollX\ is\ on,\ UNLESS\ you\ have\ specified\ a\ value\ for\ 'inner\_width'\ in\ BeginTable().}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01888\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ \ \ If\ you\ specify\ a\ value\ for\ 'inner\_width'\ then\ effectively\ the\ scrolling\ space\ is\ known\ and\ Stretch\ or\ mixed\ Fixed/Stretch\ columns\ become\ meaningful\ again.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01889\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ -\/\ Read\ on\ documentation\ at\ the\ top\ of\ imgui\_tables.cpp\ for\ details.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01890\ \textcolor{keyword}{enum}\ ImGuiTableFlags\_}
\DoxyCodeLine{01891\ \{}

\DoxyCodeLine{01913\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ Sizing\ Policy\ (read\ above\ for\ defaults)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01914\ \ \ \ \ ImGuiTableFlags\_SizingFixedFit\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ =\ 1\ <<\ 13,\ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ Columns\ default\ to\ \_WidthFixed\ or\ \_WidthAuto\ (if\ resizable\ or\ not\ resizable),\ matching\ contents\ width.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01915\ \ \ \ \ ImGuiTableFlags\_SizingFixedSame\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ =\ 2\ <<\ 13,\ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ Columns\ default\ to\ \_WidthFixed\ or\ \_WidthAuto\ (if\ resizable\ or\ not\ resizable),\ matching\ the\ maximum\ contents\ width\ of\ all\ columns.\ Implicitly\ enable\ ImGuiTableFlags\_NoKeepColumnsVisible.}}

\DoxyCodeLine{02286\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ -\/\ Recovery\ after\ running\ an\ exception\ handler\ or\ any\ error\ processing\ which\ may\ skip\ code\ after\ an\ error\ has\ been\ detected.}}

\DoxyCodeLine{02290\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ -\/\ By\ design,\ we\ do\ NOT\ allow\ error\ recovery\ to\ be\ 100\%\ silent.\ One\ of\ the\ three\ options\ needs\ to\ be\ checked!}}

\DoxyCodeLine{02292\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ Otherwise\ it\ would\ severely\ hinder\ your\ ability\ to\ catch\ and\ correct\ mistakes!}}

\DoxyCodeLine{02295\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ -\/\ Non-\/programmer\ seats:\ maybe\ disable\ asserts,\ but\ make\ sure\ errors\ are\ resurfaced\ (tooltips,\ visible\ log\ entries,\ use\ callback\ etc.)}}

\DoxyCodeLine{02611\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ This\ is\ optimized\ for\ efficient\ lookup\ (dichotomy\ into\ a\ contiguous\ buffer)\ and\ rare\ insertion\ (typically\ tied\ to\ user\ interactions\ aka\ max\ once\ a\ frame)}}

\DoxyCodeLine{02621\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ -\/\ Get***()\ functions\ find\ pair,\ never\ add/allocate.\ Pairs\ are\ sorted\ so\ a\ query\ is\ O(log\ N)}}

\DoxyCodeLine{02786\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ Multi-\/selection\ system}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02787\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ Documentation\ at:\ https://github.com/ocornut/imgui/wiki/Multi-\/Select}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02788\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ -\/\ Refer\ to\ 'Demo-\/>Widgets-\/>Selection\ State\ \&\ Multi-\/Select'\ for\ demos\ using\ this.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02789\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ -\/\ This\ system\ implements\ standard\ multi-\/selection\ idioms\ (CTRL+Mouse/Keyboard,\ SHIFT+Mouse/Keyboard,\ etc)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02790\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ with\ support\ for\ clipper\ (skipping\ non-\/visible\ items),\ box-\/select\ and\ many\ other\ details.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02791\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ -\/\ Selectable(),\ Checkbox()\ are\ supported\ but\ custom\ widgets\ may\ use\ it\ as\ well.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02792\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ -\/\ TreeNode()\ is\ technically\ supported\ but...\ using\ this\ correctly\ is\ more\ complicated:\ you\ need\ some\ sort\ of\ linear/random\ access\ to\ your\ tree,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02793\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ which\ is\ suited\ to\ advanced\ trees\ setups\ also\ implementing\ filters\ and\ clipper.\ We\ will\ work\ toward\ simplifying\ and\ demoing\ it.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02794\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ -\/\ In\ the\ spirit\ of\ Dear\ ImGui\ design,\ your\ code\ owns\ actual\ selection\ data.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02795\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ This\ is\ designed\ to\ allow\ all\ kinds\ of\ selection\ storage\ you\ may\ use\ in\ your\ application\ e.g.\ set/map/hash.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02796\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ About\ ImGuiSelectionBasicStorage:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02797\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ -\/\ This\ is\ an\ optional\ helper\ to\ store\ a\ selection\ state\ and\ apply\ selection\ requests.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02798\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ -\/\ It\ is\ used\ by\ our\ demos\ and\ provided\ as\ a\ convenience\ to\ quickly\ implement\ multi-\/selection.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02799\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ Usage:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02800\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ -\/\ Identify\ submitted\ items\ with\ SetNextItemSelectionUserData(),\ most\ likely\ using\ an\ index\ into\ your\ current\ data-\/set.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02801\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ -\/\ Store\ and\ maintain\ actual\ selection\ data\ using\ persistent\ object\ identifiers.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02802\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ -\/\ Usage\ flow:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02803\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ \ BEGIN\ -\/\ (1)\ Call\ BeginMultiSelect()\ and\ retrieve\ the\ ImGuiMultiSelectIO*\ result.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02804\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ -\/\ (2)\ Honor\ request\ list\ (SetAll/SetRange\ requests)\ by\ updating\ your\ selection\ data.\ Same\ code\ as\ Step\ 6.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02805\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ -\/\ (3)\ [If\ using\ clipper]\ You\ need\ to\ make\ sure\ RangeSrcItem\ is\ always\ submitted.\ Calculate\ its\ index\ and\ pass\ to\ clipper.IncludeItemByIndex().\ If\ storing\ indices\ in\ ImGuiSelectionUserData,\ a\ simple\ clipper.IncludeItemByIndex(ms\_io-\/>RangeSrcItem)\ call\ will\ work.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02806\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ \ LOOP\ \ -\/\ (4)\ Submit\ your\ items\ with\ SetNextItemSelectionUserData()\ +\ Selectable()/TreeNode()\ calls.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02807\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ \ END\ \ \ -\/\ (5)\ Call\ EndMultiSelect()\ and\ retrieve\ the\ ImGuiMultiSelectIO*\ result.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02808\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ -\/\ (6)\ Honor\ request\ list\ (SetAll/SetRange\ requests)\ by\ updating\ your\ selection\ data.\ Same\ code\ as\ Step\ 2.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02809\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ \ If\ you\ submit\ all\ items\ (no\ clipper),\ Step\ 2\ and\ 3\ are\ optional\ and\ will\ be\ handled\ by\ each\ item\ themselves.\ It\ is\ fine\ to\ always\ honor\ those\ steps.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02810\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ About\ ImGuiSelectionUserData:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02811\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ -\/\ This\ can\ store\ an\ application-\/defined\ identifier\ (e.g.\ index\ or\ pointer)\ submitted\ via\ SetNextItemSelectionUserData().}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02812\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ -\/\ In\ return\ we\ store\ them\ into\ RangeSrcItem/RangeFirstItem/RangeLastItem\ and\ other\ fields\ in\ ImGuiMultiSelectIO.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02813\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ -\/\ Most\ applications\ will\ store\ an\ object\ INDEX,\ hence\ the\ chosen\ name\ and\ type.\ Storing\ an\ index\ is\ natural,\ because}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02814\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ SetRange\ requests\ will\ give\ you\ two\ end-\/points\ and\ you\ will\ need\ to\ iterate/interpolate\ between\ them\ to\ update\ your\ selection.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02815\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ -\/\ However\ it\ is\ perfectly\ possible\ to\ store\ a\ POINTER\ or\ another\ IDENTIFIER\ inside\ ImGuiSelectionUserData.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02816\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ Our\ system\ never\ assume\ that\ you\ identify\ items\ by\ indices,\ it\ never\ attempts\ to\ interpolate\ between\ two\ values.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02817\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ -\/\ If\ you\ enable\ ImGuiMultiSelectFlags\_NoRangeSelect\ then\ it\ is\ guaranteed\ that\ you\ will\ never\ have\ to\ interpolate}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02818\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ between\ two\ ImGuiSelectionUserData,\ which\ may\ be\ a\ convenient\ way\ to\ use\ part\ of\ the\ feature\ with\ less\ code\ work.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02819\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ -\/\ As\ most\ users\ will\ want\ to\ store\ an\ index,\ for\ convenience\ and\ to\ reduce\ confusion\ we\ use\ ImS64\ instead\ of\ void*,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02820\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ being\ syntactically\ easier\ to\ downcast.\ Feel\ free\ to\ reinterpret\_cast\ and\ store\ a\ pointer\ inside.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02821\ }
\DoxyCodeLine{02822\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ Flags\ for\ BeginMultiSelect()}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02823\ \textcolor{keyword}{enum}\ ImGuiMultiSelectFlags\_}
\DoxyCodeLine{02824\ \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{02825\ \ \ \ \ ImGuiMultiSelectFlags\_None\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ =\ 0,}
\DoxyCodeLine{02826\ \ \ \ \ ImGuiMultiSelectFlags\_SingleSelect\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ =\ 1\ <<\ 0,\ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ Disable\ selecting\ more\ than\ one\ item.\ This\ is\ available\ to\ allow\ single-\/selection\ code\ to\ share\ same\ code/logic\ if\ desired.\ It\ essentially\ disables\ the\ main\ purpose\ of\ BeginMultiSelect()\ tho!}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02827\ \ \ \ \ ImGuiMultiSelectFlags\_NoSelectAll\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ =\ 1\ <<\ 1,\ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ Disable\ CTRL+A\ shortcut\ to\ select\ all.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02828\ \ \ \ \ ImGuiMultiSelectFlags\_NoRangeSelect\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ =\ 1\ <<\ 2,\ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ Disable\ Shift+selection\ mouse/keyboard\ support\ (useful\ for\ unordered\ 2D\ selection).\ With\ BoxSelect\ is\ also\ ensure\ contiguous\ SetRange\ requests\ are\ not\ combined\ into\ one.\ This\ allows\ not\ handling\ interpolation\ in\ SetRange\ requests.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02829\ \ \ \ \ ImGuiMultiSelectFlags\_NoAutoSelect\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ =\ 1\ <<\ 3,\ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ Disable\ selecting\ items\ when\ navigating\ (useful\ for\ e.g.\ supporting\ range-\/select\ in\ a\ list\ of\ checkboxes).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02830\ \ \ \ \ ImGuiMultiSelectFlags\_NoAutoClear\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ =\ 1\ <<\ 4,\ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ Disable\ clearing\ selection\ when\ navigating\ or\ selecting\ another\ one\ (generally\ used\ with\ ImGuiMultiSelectFlags\_NoAutoSelect.\ useful\ for\ e.g.\ supporting\ range-\/select\ in\ a\ list\ of\ checkboxes).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02831\ \ \ \ \ ImGuiMultiSelectFlags\_NoAutoClearOnReselect\ =\ 1\ <<\ 5,\ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ Disable\ clearing\ selection\ when\ clicking/selecting\ an\ already\ selected\ item.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02832\ \ \ \ \ ImGuiMultiSelectFlags\_BoxSelect1d\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ =\ 1\ <<\ 6,\ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ Enable\ box-\/selection\ with\ same\ width\ and\ same\ x\ pos\ items\ (e.g.\ full\ row\ Selectable()).\ Box-\/selection\ works\ better\ with\ little\ bit\ of\ spacing\ between\ items\ hit-\/box\ in\ order\ to\ be\ able\ to\ aim\ at\ empty\ space.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02833\ \ \ \ \ ImGuiMultiSelectFlags\_BoxSelect2d\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ =\ 1\ <<\ 7,\ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ Enable\ box-\/selection\ with\ varying\ width\ or\ varying\ x\ pos\ items\ support\ (e.g.\ different\ width\ labels,\ or\ 2D\ layout/grid).\ This\ is\ slower:\ alters\ clipping\ logic\ so\ that\ e.g.\ horizontal\ movements\ will\ update\ selection\ of\ normally\ clipped\ items.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02834\ \ \ \ \ ImGuiMultiSelectFlags\_BoxSelectNoScroll\ \ \ \ \ =\ 1\ <<\ 8,\ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ Disable\ scrolling\ when\ box-\/selecting\ near\ edges\ of\ scope.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02835\ \ \ \ \ ImGuiMultiSelectFlags\_ClearOnEscape\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ =\ 1\ <<\ 9,\ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ Clear\ selection\ when\ pressing\ Escape\ while\ scope\ is\ focused.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02836\ \ \ \ \ ImGuiMultiSelectFlags\_ClearOnClickVoid\ \ \ \ \ \ =\ 1\ <<\ 10,\ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ Clear\ selection\ when\ clicking\ on\ empty\ location\ within\ scope.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02837\ \ \ \ \ ImGuiMultiSelectFlags\_ScopeWindow\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ =\ 1\ <<\ 11,\ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ Scope\ for\ \_BoxSelect\ and\ \_ClearOnClickVoid\ is\ whole\ window\ (Default).\ Use\ if\ BeginMultiSelect()\ covers\ a\ whole\ window\ or\ used\ a\ single\ time\ in\ same\ window.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02838\ \ \ \ \ ImGuiMultiSelectFlags\_ScopeRect\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ =\ 1\ <<\ 12,\ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ Scope\ for\ \_BoxSelect\ and\ \_ClearOnClickVoid\ is\ rectangle\ encompassing\ BeginMultiSelect()/EndMultiSelect().\ Use\ if\ BeginMultiSelect()\ is\ called\ multiple\ times\ in\ same\ window.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02839\ \ \ \ \ ImGuiMultiSelectFlags\_SelectOnClick\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ =\ 1\ <<\ 13,\ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ Apply\ selection\ on\ mouse\ down\ when\ clicking\ on\ unselected\ item.\ (Default)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02840\ \ \ \ \ ImGuiMultiSelectFlags\_SelectOnClickRelease\ \ =\ 1\ <<\ 14,\ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ Apply\ selection\ on\ mouse\ release\ when\ clicking\ an\ unselected\ item.\ Allow\ dragging\ an\ unselected\ item\ without\ altering\ selection.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02841\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//ImGuiMultiSelectFlags\_RangeSelect2d\ \ \ \ \ \ \ =\ 1\ <<\ 15,\ \ //\ Shift+Selection\ uses\ 2d\ geometry\ instead\ of\ linear\ sequence,\ so\ possible\ to\ use\ Shift+up/down\ to\ select\ vertically\ in\ grid.\ Analogous\ to\ what\ BoxSelect\ does.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02842\ \ \ \ \ ImGuiMultiSelectFlags\_NavWrapX\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ =\ 1\ <<\ 16,\ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ [Temporary]\ Enable\ navigation\ wrapping\ on\ X\ axis.\ Provided\ as\ a\ convenience\ because\ we\ don't\ have\ a\ design\ for\ the\ general\ Nav\ API\ for\ this\ yet.\ When\ the\ more\ general\ feature\ be\ public\ we\ may\ obsolete\ this\ flag\ in\ favor\ of\ new\ one.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02843\ \};}

\DoxyCodeLine{02861\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ Selection\ request\ type}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02862\ \textcolor{keyword}{enum}\ ImGuiSelectionRequestType}

\DoxyCodeLine{02880\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ Optional\ helper\ to\ store\ multi-\/selection\ state\ +\ apply\ multi-\/selection\ requests.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02881\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ -\/\ Used\ by\ our\ demos\ and\ provided\ as\ a\ convenience\ to\ easily\ implement\ basic\ multi-\/selection.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02882\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ -\/\ Iterate\ selection\ with\ 'void*\ it\ =\ NULL;\ ImGuiID\ id;\ while\ (selection.GetNextSelectedItem(\&it,\ \&id))\ \{\ ...\ \}'}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02883\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ Or\ you\ can\ check\ 'if\ (Contains(id))\ \{\ ...\ \}'\ for\ each\ possible\ object\ if\ their\ number\ is\ not\ too\ high\ to\ iterate.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02884\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ -\/\ USING\ THIS\ IS\ NOT\ MANDATORY.\ This\ is\ only\ a\ helper\ and\ not\ a\ required\ API.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02885\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ To\ store\ a\ multi-\/selection,\ in\ your\ application\ you\ could:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02886\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ -\/\ Use\ this\ helper\ as\ a\ convenience.\ We\ use\ our\ simple\ key-\/>value\ ImGuiStorage\ as\ a\ std::set<ImGuiID>\ replacement.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02887\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ -\/\ Use\ your\ own\ external\ storage:\ e.g.\ std::set<MyObjectId>,\ std::vector<MyObjectId>,\ interval\ trees,\ intrusively\ stored\ selection\ etc.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02888\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ In\ ImGuiSelectionBasicStorage\ we:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02889\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ -\/\ always\ use\ indices\ in\ the\ multi-\/selection\ API\ (passed\ to\ SetNextItemSelectionUserData(),\ retrieved\ in\ ImGuiMultiSelectIO)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02890\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ -\/\ use\ the\ AdapterIndexToStorageId()\ indirection\ layer\ to\ abstract\ how\ persistent\ selection\ data\ is\ derived\ from\ an\ index.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02891\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ -\/\ use\ decently\ optimized\ logic\ to\ allow\ queries\ and\ insertion\ of\ very\ large\ selection\ sets.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02892\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ -\/\ do\ not\ preserve\ selection\ order.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02893\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ Many\ combinations\ are\ possible\ depending\ on\ how\ you\ prefer\ to\ store\ your\ items\ and\ how\ you\ prefer\ to\ store\ your\ selection.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02894\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ Large\ applications\ are\ likely\ to\ eventually\ want\ to\ get\ rid\ of\ this\ indirection\ layer\ and\ do\ their\ own\ thing.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02895\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ See\ https://github.com/ocornut/imgui/wiki/Multi-\/Select\ for\ details\ and\ pseudo-\/code\ using\ this\ helper.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02896\ \textcolor{keyword}{struct\ }\mbox{\hyperlink{struct_im_gui_selection_basic_storage}{ImGuiSelectionBasicStorage}}}
